### **Unknown** - 2015-11-14 18:14:29

1 lb of ground beef
1 onion chopped
1 garlic clove chopped
1 green bell pepper chopped
1 can of tomato sauce
1 can of tomato soup 
1 can of black beans
1 can of pinto beans
1 can of red kidney beans
1 can of corn
1/2 tsp of dried basil
2 tbsp of brown sugar 
2 tsp. Chili powder


### **Unknown** - 2015-11-14 18:14:57

Cook beef, onion, bell pepper, and garlic on skillet 

### **Unknown** - 2015-11-14 18:15:14

Then mix that with all other ingredients in a large pot

### **Unknown** - 2015-11-14 18:15:29

Heat and stir as long as you want

### **Unknown** - 2015-11-14 18:15:49

Make sure you strain beans

### **Unknown** - 2015-11-14 18:16:31

When you add tomato soup make sure you fill the can with water and add that too
